1538162881236< /date>
<rate>5</rate>< Review>
Based on reviews, I took my kids here. Right when we walked in we were greeted and asked what we were looking for. There were plenty of barber chairs, about 10, and we got right in. This was the day before school started and I was glad to get in so quickly. Two boys got $20 fades w/line-up. Older son got a little longer top style that was also $20. After being there for a minute I noticed the shampoo station and inquired about my daughter also getting her hair done. Miss Cherry was available and willing, she even went to the store and got the EZBraid hair. For cornrows with added hair, a few bangs and two rows at the back of the neck, $80. She added the decorations for free. There were bathrooms and parking available. My boys had to sit while their sister had her hair done, but everyone was very nice and understanding.
Fast forward a few days, my daughter has small red bumps on her scalp and has scratched it raw in a few areas. So I called and was told to bring her in and Miss Cherry would look at it. She put some aloe gel and some anti-itch scalp oil throughout the scalp and suggested to continue doing so. The style lasted three weeks. So I am happy.</Review>

< Review>
Came here with a group of coworkers after eating in Chinatown. I got the earl grey milk tea 70% sweet regular size (17oz). I didn't really like my drink because it tasted really watered down and I couldn't really taste the tea flavor but all my coworkers liked their drinks so maybe it's just a preference. Very cute logo with the regular cup size even shaped similar to a stubby/chubby little corgi butt (I'm sure that was intentional). They have a cute interior as well but it's a pretty small shop located across from the park near Chinatown. At the end of the day, the drink is most important to me and this just didn't cut it.

Workers were very nice, also nice enough to take a group picture for us but I don't see myself purposely coming back here (prices are pretty high for mediocre drinks) unless my friends or coworkers wanted to come here. In which case, I would give it another chance and try the jasmine milk tea or the roasted oolong tea. For now, I will pass on coming back.< /Review>

< text>
This place has just about EVERYTHING you'd need. Trouble is, there's such terrible service.

I stopped by to look at plastic rods. They are way high up so you can't feel them or handle them to test weight or flexibility in your hand. You have to guess. There are two buildings separated by an open lot where random trucks and forklifts come n go.

In the East building I waited and waited for someone to assist. While I waited, there was an employee screaming at someone (the owner??) about something. She was screaming. That's not hyperbole. Screaming. I was shocked. A shy man approached me and was nice and said I could look at rods in the West building. So I did.

There appeared to be 4-5 guys who looked like employees standing around. I asked for help and one grunted with his arm outstretched pointing to a desk in the next room. I took the cue and looked for help "over there". Being my first time, I must have asked too many questions because the guy working the counter was less than happy. So I bought what I thought i needed: 3 rods.  I didn't know they wouldn't work for me until AFTER I paid and i waited another 10 minutes for a worker to bring them down from a scissor lift.

When i realized it I asked for a switch  or exchange. The man said no. I asked for a refund. The man said no. So i took the rods to the car and realized there is a restocking fee with returns.

So I went back and was denied service.

I really wish this experience was for a gag show or some comedic relief, but I'm still waiting for the punch line.

I can't urge you to stay away enough unless you know that you know that you know what you're getting is going to be 100000% perfect for your needs and you honestly don't care about the negative vibes.

Good luck out there!</text>

<rating>1</rating>< review>
I have been a customer of Gavrieli for over 20 years. Our company has had an account for the past 7 years. Customer service is mixed bag, either very helpful, or the complete opposite. They have several of their own knock-off versions of various substrates, most of them lesser quality with a slight decrease in price. They used to have an edge on the competition with pricing, but that is no longer the case. The warehouse guys have absolutely no concern for the products they are giving you, every order must be thoroughly inspected. We have paid dearly for not inspecting every single sheet. One of the worst experiences we had was receiving a piece of 3/8‚Äù material that had clear film on one side. Because the protective layer was clear, we did not notice it was missing until it was back at our shop. When we called to see what could be done about the $400+ sheet I now needed to replace, the owner told me there was no way the warehouse would give us something like that. I politely asked him to take a look at our account to verify that over the previous years we have done well over $250,000 in business with them. He told me that was of no concern and I could take my business elsewhere. After this experience I have made every effort to seek out new vendors and although they may be further away, the service and quality of products is better in every regard no matter where we go.  There is such high turnover at the sales counter that product knowledge is minimal at best. If you have to use Gavrieli, it really should be a last resort. Other vendors I would highly recommend

<review>STAY AWAY FROM THIS COMPANY!!!
Worst customer service I've received from a supplier. I spoke to their sales person, Alex, for at least 20 minutes trying to order 3 items. He didn't know or understand aluminum thicknesses, so he kept putting me on hold while he "checked". Almost like he didn't know any of the items they sell. I had some downtime, so I didn't try to pressure him because I assumed he might be new at this job. I also ordered painted 4'x8' MDF, cut into (4) 12" x 8ft panels. Now, I'm having to explain the cut math. He tells me that each cut is $5(but I end up getting charged $10 on the invoice), so I tell him that he needs to charge me for 3 cuts to yield the 4 panels I need. I've ordered materials from them before, and their customer service has always been mediocre, so I continued the order because I needed the MDF. The delay to this simple order, was to due  in part to Alex writing everything down. But I remained patient because I really thought it might be his first day.
My order is scheduled for delivery the next day, but It doesn't come until the following day. The worst part is that the painted MDF that I ordered came unfinished and cut into (3) 12"x8ft, (1) 9.5"x8ft, (1) 3"x8ft. Aside from that some of the panels are bashed in around the edges and completely unusable.
I call them first thing the next day. We go  back and fourth on the phone because apparently only Alex can help me fix the order because only he and I know what was discussed. But, he's busy so I'm told he'll call me back. Its late afternoon, and I still haven' received a call.  I call them and I'm told that Alex is out to lunch and won't be back until 4pm.
I ask to be transferred to the owner after I'm told that no one can adjust or correct the invoice, except for him. So, why did I need to talk to Alex???
After talking to the owner, its abundantly obvious that the terrible customer service stems from the top. This guy clearly has no concept of what it means to treat your customers with respect. He tells me that he can't help me because the material has already been cut.I told him I agreed with that, but that unfinished MDF wasn't what I ordered. I asked him to refer to the invoice that indicated the MDF to be painted. He said, "That's what you told the guy to write on the invoice. If you're a sign-maker you should know how the material come." I then told him that it wasn't cut correctly either. Again he says, " I can't help you buddy. The transaction has already batched."
I'm not sure how this company remains in business with this kind of order resolution.<//review><GmapID>0x80c294296d9521ad:0xadb534a86115ebb8< /GmapID></record>

< review>
Nice little spot off of the freeway. There's parking so that's already a bonus.

The restaurant itself isn't that large. I didn't really explore it, but it's a decent size. We initially had a really large group, but half of us ended up coming in later.

The staff is friendly and it feels like a family run business. We ordered a special order and it was huge. There were 14 of us and the food was plentiful.

I originally wasn't set on eating kbbq. I was craving some naengmyeon, and I was dead set on ordering that. Glad I did though. It was so good!! The bowl was huge and the price was just right.

I had some kbbq and it was pretty good. Nice flavors and sliced perfectly. Well worth the money.

I almost got burned by the flames, and that was no bueno, but no fault of the restaurant. I do wish their tongs were a little bit longer, though.< /review>

<text>My favorite thing about Luiseno Park is the rock piles all along the path and behind the tennis courts. There is a huge variety of rock sizes that you can climb, jump, and hide behind or around.
The playground is great but does not have shade or swings.
Weekends it's just one big party. It always amazes me how bad it gets trashed. I feel bad for the city workers but they do an amazing job at making it beautiful by Monday late morning or afternoon.
It is safe during the day but I am not sure how safe it is a night because I have found tagging of gang symbols on trees, rocks and the playground. You wouldn't know it for the city cleans it up within a week or two.
There are 2 ball fields that can double as soccer fields, a couple picnic tables, 2 or 3 built in coal grills for BBQing, and a loop that is wonderful for biking and walking.< /text>< gmap_id>

<Text>My kids and I love this park. It's a bit off the beaten path so if you don't know about it or frequent the back gate or Mainside gate to Camp Pendleton you may never know it's there. I've been taking my kids here for probably ten years and it's still one of the best and safest parks around. The park is a great size for a neighborhood park with lots or green space for the kids and pets. Two baseball or softball diamonds and a decent playground area for smaller kids up to 10 or so. For adults or your older teens, there is also enclosed tennis court if that's your thing. The only thing that keeps this place from receiving five stars is the inconsistent cleanliness of the bathroom. Some days, they're clean but most days not so much.  Obviously, it's a public park so you can't expect them to be spotless but sometimes they are really dirty and not appropriate for small kids.</Text>< pictures>

<Rating>3<//Rating><Text>I love the location of this park in proximity to my home. My daughters love to come here also.

The Pros:

Benches to sit outside to watch your kids play.

There are grills if you want to come out and cook, play or just hang out. A plus for birthday party's or summer.

There are two baseball diamonds out where  there are regular games going on. You can also come out to practice.

The Cons:

There is no outside lighting by the picnic area or playground . This is a potential threat to people being out here who aren't with a crowd of people. Even in the area where the bleachers are located it is not lighted. Once the baseball field lights turn off, the park is pitch black!!

The bathrooms look like a scary movie inside. Please BYO soap and sanitizer. They're never stocked with tissue and soap
OR towels to dry your hands. The garbage cans are also outside of the restrooms.

The playground is extremely basic for the amount of space this park has. It is not colorful and there are no swings (at a park) I'd suggest that the city add swings and more activities for the children to do to stay busy. Overall, it's a nice place to come to- it just needs these things to be rectified.<//Text><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< user_id>

Tara Gooden< /Name>
<date>1525583869488</date><Rate>4<//Rate>< review>
This is specifically for the Soquel Avenue location. This is one of the best taquerias in town and I'm always amazed that it doesn't make the "best of" lists published. The carna asada has SO much flavor. The tacos are delicious and packed full of meat. I'd highly recommend the carne asada tacos, any variety of the super burritos (but especially the shrimp), the cheese enchiladas, and the tostado. Prices are fairly reasonable, but they've gone up lately. Parking is easy to find and the restaurant itself is huge with plenty of tables. They have a salsa bar with amazing pico de gayo and serve fresh chips with every order. There's a selection of Mexican beverages and desserts. The interior is a little worn, and some menu items are pricier than others. Really love this place.</review>

< review>
Reading these reviews I have come to the following conclusions:
1. This place has excellent tacos. Order them.
2. Get the Al Pastor as your meat choice.
3. Don't order veggie here. (Or at any taqueria really. I mean c'mon.)
4. If you're acting privileged you will be treated accordingly. Smile and be respectful.
5. Be prepared to spend a little more than you'd like, but the Al Pastor tacos will make you glad you did.
6. If all else fails order the soup. The soup is the best thing on the menu.
7. Whatever you order get it to go, make sure to check it over before you leave, like any thinking person would.
Enjoy!<//review>

< Review>
Arguably, one of the best Mexican joints in all of Santa Cruz. I never had a bad experience here. Food is great for its price. What really helps this place stand out is its "Carne en su jugo", a beef stew served with avocado, beans, and a delicious broth. I enjoy savoring it's succulent flavor and with spicy foods, even better. Typically, I put some chili peppers with my stew. Overall, a great place to get some delicious Mexican food.<//Review>

< Review>
The service can be a little surly and gruff, but the food is fantastic. Taqueria Santa Cruz has some favorites that you just can't get in other taquerias, like birria (bbq goat), carne en su jugo (beef soup), and camarones en mojo de ajo (shrimp in garlic sauce). They could be a little less stingy with their chips (you only get a tiny bag with your meal) but their salsas are delicious.<//Review>

<user_id>113121546333166662211< /user_id>< username>
Karma Kali<//username>
<Time>1513663912873<//Time><Rate>1<//Rate>< review>
Lackluster service, worst vegetarian burrito I have ever had, inflated prices, gossipy environment and last time I went I found a pebble in my burrito. They replaced it but the new burrito was mostly inedible.

To be more clear, my second or third time coming to this restaurant, the woman at the cash register, who was already very unfriendly, got angry because I asked a man behind me for change so I wouldn't have to break my last twenty. He was more than happy to supply the change but she acted like I was pan handling and told me if I ever do that again she would kick me out and I would be persona non grata. I made a review highlighting her treatment of me that day, as well as previous times where her attitude was equally unkind.

I made the mistake of going in one final time after a late night work out. I ordered the tripas burrito. I tried to be friendly and ask her how she was and I honestly asked if she had seen my review. She said she had.  I was feeling incredibly gracious and even apologized for posting it. She said it was fine and that people were even coming in telling her how great she was because of it. I was genuinely happy she was able to receive positively because of my review.

I left with my daughter and I' s food. I got inside my vehicle, took a bite and bit down on a huge pebble, and what appeared to be pieces of rocks. I brought back the burrito and asked her sincerely if it was retribution for the review I wrote. She said she was insulted by my inquiry. She said that it was normal for tripas burritos to have pebbles in them. She refused to refund my money and offered a replacement burrito.

Again, I made the mistake of going along instead of insisting on a refund. This time I chose a vegetarian burrito, hoping it would be pebble free. I even kept glancing at the guys making it. It was the worst burrito I had ever tasted. Maybe some folks like feta and lettuce galore in their burrito but not me! It got tossed, even though I normally don't waste food.

As an empath and  single mom of three, I feel everything deeply. Kindness and lack thereof. In a way, the unkindness serves me too, because it has taught me deep, tearful  gratitide for kindness and people who choose kindness. This place has taught me deep gratitude for good food (pebble free), good service, and of course, kindness. May we all choose more and more kindness, especially since we all depend on it.

I hope this helps and thank you for reading.< /review>
